< text>
OC is known for beautiful beach fronts and  Newport is one of the best spots for a nice cool breeze by a short amusing ferry trip! You will be hopping from the island side (it is called 'Balboa island') to the Peninsula for about 5 to 7 min. ride on a small fleet that can carry up to 3 mid sized cars and 20 to 30 people at a time. It only costs a buck or two per person and a little more for an automobile. On the Peninsula side, there are things to ride as you may see from a small village festival such as wheel ride and also many restuarants for pizza or burgers.< /text>

< Text>
Such a beautiful place to visit it's like a postcard. Ride the ferry across to the Fun Zone then take a nice stroll down to the pier and get some Ruby's Diner. You can then ride your bike up and down the boardwalk or go fishing off the pier or just lay on the sand and relax with your toes in the water. <username>Plimsoul</username><date>1560313346769</date>< rating>
4</rating>
< Text>
Great short ferry between Balboa Island and Balboa Peninsula...love walking the area and taking the ferry back and forth. Only $1 per ride for pedestrians, and $1.25 if you have a bike. I think $1.50 for motorcyles and $2.00 for a vehicle and driver plus $1.00 extras for each adult passagers. Kids under 5 are free and kids 5 thru 11 are $.50. It's a bargain transport. Ferry runs until 2 am on Friday and Saturday and until 12 am Sunday thru Thursday. You pay your fare after you get on the boat.<//Text>
